# Text Elements
Strength of Acid ^8W16uyp8

Is always dependant on it's Ability to Dissociate in to IONS ^H8rq9KPW

Strength in acidity is dependant on how EASILY H+ is formed

-> Completely dissociate into H+-> Strong Acid
-> Partially dissociate into H+-> Weak Acids ^AvBfQUqW
